agot_spawn_canon_cradle_dragon_effect = {
	$CRADLEMATE$ = { save_scope_as = owner }
	if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_13_b = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_anogaros_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_13_d = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_archonei_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_belaerys_1 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_terrax_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_21 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_meraxes_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_30 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_quicksilver_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_35 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_vermithor_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_36 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_silverwing_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_velaryon_35 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_seasmoke_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_75 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_vermax_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_76 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_arrax_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_77 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_tyraxes_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_78 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_stormcloud_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_69 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_moondancer_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_70 = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = hatched_wyrmling }
			agot_spawn_morning_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			agot_spawn_rhaena_1_effect = yes
			scope:dragon = {
				trigger_event = { id = agot_dragon.9000 days = 1 }
			}
			remove_character_flag = hatched_canon_dragon
			add_character_flag = hatched_wyrmling
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_72 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_shrykos_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_71 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_morghul_effect = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_velaryon_44 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_laena_1_effect = yes
		#needs murder events
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_74 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_nightfyre_effect = yes
		#needs murder events
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			scope:owner = { is_character_targaryen_9 = yes }
		}
		agot_spawn_drogon_effect = yes
	}
	else = {
		create_character = {
			location = scope:owner.location
			template = agot_dragon_hatchling_template
			random_traits = no
			save_scope_as = dragon
		}
	}
}

agot_set_reserved_canon_egg_scope = {
	$EGG$ = { save_scope_as = egg }
	if = {
		limit = { agot_is_valid_vhagar_birth = { EGG = scope:egg } }
		save_scope_as = vhagar_birth_reserved
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { agot_is_valid_serporoth_birth = { EGG = scope:egg } }
		save_scope_as = serporoth_birth_reserved
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { agot_is_valid_cannibal_birth = { EGG = scope:egg } }

#just to keep track of dragons that weren't cradle or pit
agot_spawn_random_historical_dragon = {
	random_list = {
		1 = { agot_spawn_nagga_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_urrax_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_ancestor_5_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_ancestor_1_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_ancestor_6_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_ancestor_2_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_vassarion_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_essovius_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_valryon_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_ghiscar_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_vermithrax_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_balerion_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_nessarion_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_ancestor_3_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_ancestor_3_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_rovax_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_ancestor_4_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_neltharion_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_pythax_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_rhaegal_effect = yes }
		1 = { agot_spawn_viserion_effect = yes }
	}
}

agot_spawn_nagga_effect = {  # (History id = dragon_nagga)
	create_character = {
		name = "Nagga"
		gender = female
		culture = culture:dragon_culture
		faith = faith:valyrian_pan_freehold
		location = scope:owner.location
		age = 0
		#mother = character:UNKNOWN
		dynasty = none
		trait = dragon
		trait = dragon_physique_good_3

		random_traits = no
		save_scope_as = dragon

		# Nagga
		after_creation = {
			make_trait_inactive = is_dragon_nagga

			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_gender_hidden
				value = 1
			}

			create_story = story_dragon_alive

			# Needed for visuals
			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_age
				value = age
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_size
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_size_base
				value = 0
			}

			agot_back_apply_dragon_aging_effect = yes

			# Dragon Appearance
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_primary_color_hue
				value = 0.34
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_metallic_scales_strength
				value = 0.0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_wounded
				value = 0.0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_body_shading_template
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_body_shading_value
				value = 0.0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_wings_shading_template
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_wings_shading_value
				value = 0.0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_primary_color_value
				value = 0.57
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_secondary_hue
				value = 1.00
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_tertiary_hue
				value = 0.00
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_tertiary_value
				value = 0.00
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_secondary_value
				value = 0.62
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_eye_color_hue
				value = 0.27
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_eye_color_value
				value = 0.55
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_horn_color_hue
				value = 0.74
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_horn_color_value
				value = 0.18
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_brow_width
				value = 0.89
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_cheek_width
				value = 0.68
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_chin_profile
				value = 0.89
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_crest_depth
				value = 0.21
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_head_roundness
				value = 0.34
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_horns_eyebrow_length
				value = 0.32
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_main_horn_shape_value
				value = 0.36
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_main_horn_shape_template
				value = 2
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_jaw_width
				value = 0.48
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_lower_jaw_height
				value = 0.49
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_lower_jaw_width
				value = 0.14
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_old_neck
				value = 0.02
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_outer_brow_height
				value = 0.15
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_snout_height
				value = 0.56
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_snout_length
				value = 0.26
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_snout_profile
				value = 0.36
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_snout_width
				value = 0.36
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_upper_jaw_width
				value = 0.04
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_back_spike_size
				value = 0.88
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_center_fin_size
				value = 0.13
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_horns_eyebrow
				value = 0.35
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_neck_spike_size
				value = 0.73
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_side_fin_size
				value = 0.97
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_snout_end_width
				value = 0.30
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_neck_length
				value = 0.00
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_tail_length
				value = 0.65
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = primary_color_grading
				value = flag:middle
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = primary_color
				value = flag:green
			}

			agot_dragon_transfer_vars_to_story_cycle_effect = { DRAGON = scope:dragon }

			#Stop current egg from being reforged
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:egg
				}
				scope:egg = {
					set_variable = { name = currently_hatching }
				}
			}
			agot_dragon_birth_magic_effect = yes

			#Canon Traits
			if = {
				limit = { has_game_rule = agot_canon_dragons_enabled_traits }

				add_character_flag = agot_canon_education_dragon_1

				add_character_flag = agot_developing_canon_dragon_traits
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0002 # dragon_aggressive
					years = 3
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.9998
					years = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
agot_spawn_urrax_effect = {  # (History id = dragon_urrax)
	create_character = {
		name = "Urrax"
		gender = male
		culture = culture:dragon_culture
		faith = faith:valyrian_pan_freehold
		location = scope:owner.location
		age = 0
		#mother = character:UNKNOWN
		dynasty = none
		trait = dragon

		random_traits = no
		save_scope_as = dragon

		# Urrax
		after_creation = {
			make_trait_inactive = is_dragon_urrax

			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_gender_hidden
				value = 1
			}

			create_story = story_dragon_alive

			# Needed for visuals
			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_age
				value = age
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_size
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_size_base
				value = 0
			}

			agot_back_apply_dragon_aging_effect = yes

			# Dragon Appearance
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_primary_color_value
				value = 0.45
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_secondary_hue
				value = 0.42
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_tertiary_hue
				value = 0.00
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_tertiary_value
				value = 0.00
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_secondary_value
				value = 0.91
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_eye_color_hue
				value = 0.86
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_eye_color_value
				value = 0.16
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_horn_color_hue
				value = 0.50
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_horn_color_value
				value = 0.76
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_brow_width
				value = 0.39
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_cheek_width
				value = 0.94
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_chin_profile
				value = 0.55
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_crest_depth
				value = 0.55
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_head_roundness
				value = 0.60
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_horns_eyebrow_length
				value = 0.77
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_main_horn_shape_template
				value = 6
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_main_horn_shape_value
				value = 0.20
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_jaw_width
				value = 0.84
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_lower_jaw_height
				value = 0.71
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_lower_jaw_width
				value = 0.65
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_old_neck
				value = 0.88
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_outer_brow_height
				value = 0.43
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_snout_height
				value = 0.76
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_snout_length
				value = 0.94
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_snout_profile
				value = 0.25
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_snout_width
				value = 0.41
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_upper_jaw_width
				value = 0.62
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_center_fin_size
				value = 0.63
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_back_spike_size
				value = 0.12
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_horns_eyebrow
				value = 0.45
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_neck_spike_size
				value = 0.60
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_side_fin_size
				value = 0.27
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_snout_end_width
				value = 0.98
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_neck_length
				value = 0.23
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_tail_length
				value = 0.45
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_primary_color_hue
				value = 0.76
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_metallic_scales_strength
				value = 0.0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_wounded
				value = 0.0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_body_shading_template
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_body_shading_value
				value = 0.0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_wings_shading_template
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_wings_shading_value
				value = 0.0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = primary_color_grading
				value = flag:middle
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = primary_color
				value = flag:purple
			}

			agot_dragon_transfer_vars_to_story_cycle_effect = { DRAGON = scope:dragon }

			#Stop current egg from being reforged
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:egg
				}
				scope:egg = {
					set_variable = { name = currently_hatching }
				}
			}
			agot_dragon_birth_magic_effect = yes

			#Canon Traits
			if = {
				limit = { has_game_rule = agot_canon_dragons_enabled_traits }

				add_character_flag = agot_canon_education_dragon_1

				add_character_flag = agot_developing_canon_dragon_traits
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0005 # dragon_accepting
					years = 3
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0010 # dragon_impulsive
					years = 6
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0012 # dragon_solitary
					years = 10
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.9999
					years = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
			set_variable = {
				name = primary_color
				value = flag:grey
			}

			agot_dragon_transfer_vars_to_story_cycle_effect = { DRAGON = scope:dragon }

			#Stop current egg from being reforged
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:egg
				}
				scope:egg = {
					set_variable = { name = currently_hatching }
				}
			}
			agot_dragon_birth_magic_effect = yes

			#Canon Traits
			if = {
				limit = { has_game_rule = agot_canon_dragons_enabled_traits }

				add_character_flag = agot_canon_education_dragon_2

				add_character_flag = agot_developing_canon_dragon_traits
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0002 # dragon_aggressive
					years = 3
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0014 # dragon_voracious
					years = 6
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0010 # dragon_impulsive
					years = 10
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.9999
					years = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		dynasty = none
		trait = dragon
		trait = dragon_physique_good_3

		random_traits = no
		save_scope_as = dragon

		# Balerion
		after_creation = {
			make_trait_inactive = is_dragon_balerion

			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_gender_hidden

			}
			set_variable = {

				value = 0.97
			}

				value = 0.29
			}

			}

				name = gene_dragon_primary_color_hue

				value = 0.6

				name = gene_dragon_body_shading_template

				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_wings_shading_value
				value = 0.0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = primary_color_grading
				value = flag:middle
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = primary_color
				value = flag:grey
			}

			agot_dragon_transfer_vars_to_story_cycle_effect = { DRAGON = scope:dragon }

			#Stop current egg from being reforged
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:egg
				}
				scope:egg = {
					set_variable = { name = currently_hatching }
				}
			}
			agot_dragon_birth_magic_effect = yes

			#Canon Traits
			if = {
				limit = { has_game_rule = agot_canon_dragons_enabled_traits }

				add_character_flag = agot_canon_education_dragon_3

				add_character_flag = agot_developing_canon_dragon_traits
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0011 # dragon_cooperative
					years = 3
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0001 # dragon_friendly
					years = 6
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0013 # dragon_restrained
					years = 10
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.9999
					years = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				add_character_flag = agot_canon_education_dragon_2

				#No canon traits
			}
		}
	}

			make_trait_inactive = dragon_fertile
			set_variable = dragon_is_fertile

			#Canon Traits
			if = {
				limit = { has_game_rule = agot_canon_dragons_enabled_traits }

				add_character_flag = agot_canon_education_dragon_4

				add_character_flag = agot_developing_canon_dragon_traits
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0009 # dragon_calculating
					years = 3
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0008 # dragon_imperious
					years = 6
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0006 # dragon_defiant
					years = 10
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.9999
					years = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			set_variable = {
				name = primary_color
				value = flag:white
			}

			agot_dragon_transfer_vars_to_story_cycle_effect = { DRAGON = scope:dragon }

			#Stop current egg from being reforged
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:egg
				}
				scope:egg = {
					set_variable = { name = currently_hatching }
				}
			}
			agot_dragon_birth_magic_effect = yes

			#Fertile
			make_trait_inactive = dragon_fertile
			set_variable = dragon_is_fertile

			#Canon Traits
			if = {
				limit = { has_game_rule = agot_canon_dragons_enabled_traits }

				add_character_flag = agot_canon_education_dragon_5

				add_character_flag = agot_developing_canon_dragon_traits
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0005 # dragon_accepting
					years = 3
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0011 # dragon_cooperative
					years = 6
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0001 # dragon_friendly
					years = 10
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.9999
					years = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				#No canon traits
			}
		}
	}

			}

			#Stop current egg from being reforged
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:egg
				}
				scope:egg = {
					set_variable = { name = currently_hatching }
				}
			}
			agot_dragon_birth_magic_effect = yes

			#Canon Traits
			if = {
				limit = { has_game_rule = agot_canon_dragons_enabled_traits }

				add_character_flag = agot_canon_education_dragon_4

				add_character_flag = agot_developing_canon_dragon_traits
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0002 # dragon_aggressive
					years = 3
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0004 # dragon_bloodthirsty
					years = 6
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0009 # dragon_calculating
					years = 10
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.9999
					years = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					years = 7
				}

		}
	}

				}

					set_variable = { name = currently_hatching }
				}
			}

				add_character_flag = agot_developing_canon_dragon_traits

					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0012 # dragon_solitary
					years = 3
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0009 # dragon_calculating
					years = 6
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0003 # dragon_skittish
					years = 10
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.9999
					years = 15
				}
			}
		}

				}

					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.9999
					years = 15
				}
			}
		}

				value = flag:middle
			}

				name = primary_color
				value = flag:grey
			}

			if = {

					exists = scope:egg
				}
				scope:egg = {
					set_variable = { name = currently_hatching }
				}
			}
			agot_dragon_birth_magic_effect = yes

				add_character_flag = agot_developing_canon_dragon_traits
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0007 # dragon_supporting
					years = 3
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0009 # dragon_calculating
					years = 6
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0012 # dragon_solitary
					years = 10
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.9999
					years = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}

				add_character_flag = agot_canon_education_dragon_3

				#No canon traits
			}
		}
	}

			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_tail_length
				value = 0.5
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = primary_color_grading
				value = flag:middle
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = primary_color
				value = flag:green
			}

			agot_dragon_transfer_vars_to_story_cycle_effect = { DRAGON = scope:dragon }

			#Stop current egg from being reforged
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:egg
				}
				scope:egg = {
					set_variable = { name = currently_hatching }
				}
			}
			agot_dragon_birth_magic_effect = yes

			#Canon Traits
			if = {
				limit = { has_game_rule = agot_canon_dragons_enabled_traits }

				add_character_flag = agot_canon_education_dragon_2

				add_character_flag = agot_developing_canon_dragon_traits
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0006 # dragon_defiant
					years = 3
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.0010 # dragon_impulsive
					years = 6
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = agot_dragon_canon_personality.9998
					years = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
agot_spawn_viserion_effect = {  # (History id = dragon_viserion)
	create_character = {
		name = "Viserion"
		gender = male
		culture = culture:dragon_culture
		faith = faith:valyrian_pan_freehold
		location = scope:owner.location
		age = 0
		mother = character:dragon_dreamfyre
		dynasty = none
		trait = dragon
		trait = dragon_destined
		trait = dragon_physique_good_2

		random_traits = no
		save_scope_as = dragon

		# Viserion
		after_creation = {
			make_trait_inactive = is_dragon_viserion

			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_gender_hidden
				value = 1
			}

			create_story = story_dragon_alive

			# Needed for visuals
			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_age
				value = age
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_size
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = dragon_size_base
				value = 0
			}

			agot_back_apply_dragon_aging_effect = yes

			# Dragon Appearance
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_primary_color_hue
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gene_dragon_metallic_scales_strength
				value = 0.15
